style="page-break-after:always"/><div style="min-height:36pt;width:100%"><div><span><br/></span></div></div><div style="margin-top:9pt;padding-left:76.5pt;text-indent:-76.5pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">Item 8.01 </span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">     </span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">  </span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">Other Events.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On October 11, 2024, Visa Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) announced new conversion rates applicable to the Company&#8217;s class B-1 and B-2 common stock resulting from its September 26, 2024 deposit of $1.5 billion into the U.S. litigation escrow account previously established under the Company&#8217;s U.S. retrospective responsibility plan (the &#8220;Plan&#8221;). Under the terms of the Plan, the conversion rate applicable to the Company&#8217;s class B-1 common stock decreased from 1.5875 to 1.5653 and the conversion rate applicable to the Company's class B-2 common stock decreased from 1.5875 to 1.5430, in each case effective as of September 26, 2024. </span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The conversion rate adjustments have the same effect on earnings per share as repurchasing the Company&#8217;s class A common stock. Therefore, the as-converted class B-1 common stock share count was reduced by approximately 107,575 from 7,676,253 to 7,568,678 and the as-converted class B-2 common stock share count was reduced by approximately 5,354,510 from 191,040,105 to 185,685,595. The deposit and conversion rate adjustment calculations were conducted in accordance with the Company&#8217;s certificate of incorporation currently in effect using the volume-weighted average price over the 13-day pricing period from September 24, 2024 through October 10, 2024.</span></div><div style="height:36pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><span><br/></span></div></div></div><div id="i32217e8a51a0428da295797bf3296c23_10"></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"/><div
